<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">B级：结构值（硬度+阈值）*3，硬度8，出力12，机动12，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">A级：结构值（硬度+阈值）*3，硬度16，出力20，机动20，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">S级：结构值（硬度+阈值）*3，硬度32，出力36，机动36，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">载具拥有：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">0/3/6/12/24/48点</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">装甲值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">*</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">某些奇怪的载具不完全按照这个规则，如钢铁侠的战甲，自行车等。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">============================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">生物模板（包括生物类载具以及召唤生物）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">生物默认同一时间只能有一个，与</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">PC一样拥有迅捷，移动，标准动作，无须召生物根据自己的先攻进行行动。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">召唤的生物直接行动则需要支付</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">1个同级特性。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">需要每轮支付额外动作操控的召唤生物，根据所需的动作获得特性补正，补正的特性仅能用于提高召唤生物：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">全回合动作：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">2个同级特性</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">整轮动作：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">1个同级特性和1个次级特性</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">标准动作：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">1个同级特性</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">移动动作：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">1个次级特性</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">迅捷动作：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">1个再次级特性</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">自由动作：不补</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">生物载具或者召唤生物的生物属性：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">召唤生物总是有</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">2个主属性，3个副属性，其他4项皆为通常属性；召唤生物有3个主技能，4个副技能，5个次技能，其他技能皆为0。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">无支线：主属性为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">5</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">，副属性为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">3</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">，通常属性为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">2</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">；主技能为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">5</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">，副技能为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">2，次技能为1，15个专长点数。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">D级：主属性为6</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">，副属性为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">3</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">，通常属性为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">2；主技能为7</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">，副技能为</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">3 ，次技能为1，30个</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255)"><font face="宋体">专长点数。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">*在购买/计算使用技能提升生物属性值所需的特性时，以D1C2B4A8S16的价格计算特性价格，并且如同血统/改造一般计算召唤物在该项属性上可获得的属性上限。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 7.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; BACKGROUND: rgb(255,255,255); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-shading: rgb(255,255,255); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><font face="宋体">*若为召唤生物，则持续时间如技能一般提供特性补正。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
